而我認為姑娘們能夠做到	and i think girls can do it .
法塔赫組織成員:我們必須清空頭腦中傳統的觀念	fatah member: we have to clear up the conventional wisdom in the mind .
哈馬斯組織成員:我們是完全和平的我們希望讓它遍及整個巴勒斯坦	hamas: we're completely peaceful , and we want it to go all the way through palestine .
口號聲:團結一致的民族	slogan: solidarity .
法塔赫哈馬斯人民陣線	the fatah hamas people's fronts .
新聞主播:圍牆附近的衝突仍在繼續	news anchor: conflicts around the wall continue .
記者:以色列邊警受命驅逐抗議人群	interviewer: israeli police deported protesters .
他們被允許採用一切必要的強制手段	they're allowed to adopt the mandates necessary .
男子:他們正在開火	man: they're on fire .
這裡就像費盧傑到處是槍聲	this is like the sound of a gunshot everywhere .
以色列行動主義者:我知道我們是去送死	israeli activist: i know we are dying .
但是我身邊的許多人沒有一絲畏懼	but many of the people around me don't fear .
以色列士兵:一場非暴力抗議無法阻止我們建立這堵牆	israeli soldier: a nonviolent protest can't stop us from building this wall .
抗議者:這是一場和平的示威遊行	protesters: this is a peaceful protest march .
我們不需要使用暴力	we don't need to use violence .
口號聲:我們必勝我們必勝	slogan: we must win .
朱莉婭•帕夏:當我第一次聽說佈德魯斯的這段故事我感到非常驚訝全球媒體居然沒有報道在2003年也就是七年以前所發生的這一系列了不起的事件	julia passha: when i first heard this story from bew russ , i was surprised that the world's media had no newspaper in 2003 , this amazing series of events that happened seven years ago .
而更令人吃驚的是佈德魯斯最終取得了勝利	and what's even more surprising is that leuce eventually won .
經過長達10個月的和平抵抗運動那裡的居民說服了以色列政府將圍牆從他們的土地遷出轉而遷到綠線上也就是國際公認的巴以領土分界線上	over the course of 10 months of peaceful resistance , where residents convinced israeli governments to migrate from their lands to the green line , the international recognition of baseline .
佈德魯斯的抵抗運動的影響從此遍及約旦河西岸的所有村莊以及耶路撒冷境內的巴勒斯坦人居住區	the impact of bulderrus' resistance has spread across all of the villages in the west bank and the palestinian settlements in jerusalem .
然而媒體對這些事件幾乎隻字未提	but the media has very little to say about these events .
這種漠視給巴勒斯坦非暴力運動的成長甚至生存產生了沉重的打擊	this indifference depends on the growth of nonviolent movements in palestine and even the survival of survival .
暴力抵抗和非暴力抵抗有一個非常重要的共同點兩者像一個劇院渴望吸引觀眾的青睞	violence resistance and nonviolent resistance have a very important common denominator: a desire to attract audiences .
如果暴力演員總是領銜主演將全球目光聚焦巴勒斯坦問題那麼非暴力領導人就很難向他們的民眾證明和平的反抗才是帶他們脫離苦海的可行方案	if violent actors are always leading the world to focus on palestinian problems , then nonviolent leaders are struggling to demonstrate peace to their citizens that it is possible to get them out of the suffering .
在座為人父母的估計對關注的力量並不陌生	the estimates for a parent are not unfamiliar with the power of attention .
如果孩子第一次鬧脾氣就得到父母的注意那麼你的孩子以後肯定會鬧得更厲害	if your child ever gets a parent's attention for the first tantrum , then your child will surely be much more awesome .
鬧脾氣就會成為兒童心理學家所說的功能性行為孩子學會用這種方式引起父母的注意	the temple becomes what a child psychologist calls functional behavior , and the child learns to catch a parent's attention in this way .
父母可以透過關注或不予理睬來鼓勵或抑制此行為	parents can encourage or inhibit that by paying attention or not giving ignored reasons .
而這也適用於成年人	and this applies to adults .
事實上社群和國家的行為是能夠受到影響而改變的而這取決於國際社會選擇關注的方面	in fact , the behavior of communities and countries can be affected and changed , depending on the international selection of international society .
我相信解決中東地區的衝突給這裡帶來和平關鍵是我們要透過更多地關注當地的非暴力領袖來把非暴力行動轉變為一種功能性行為	i believe that the key to solving conflict in the middle east is to bring peace here , and we need to take more attention to local nonviolent leaders to transform nonviolent action into a functional behavior .
在約旦河西岸加沙地帶以及東耶路撒冷地區拍攝那裡的村莊時我親眼目睹了區區一部紀錄片對行為轉變所帶來的影響	in the west banks of jordan , in the west bank , in gaza , and in east jerusalem , i saw firsthand the impact of a documentary film on behavioral transformation .
在離耶路撒冷很近的一個名叫瓦拉傑的村子那裡的村民面臨著與佈德魯斯相似的困境	in a village near jerusalem called varajo , where the villagers face a plight similar to broadrush .
他們即將被包圍起來失去大片土地無法自由進入約旦河西岸或耶路撒冷	they're going to be surrounded , lose mass of land , freedom of access to the west bank or jerusalem .
在進行了長達兩年的非暴力抵抗之後他們最終心灰意冷因為他們沒有得到任何人的注意	after two years of nonviolent resistance , they eventually frustrated because they didn't get anybody's attention .
於是我們在那裡組織播放了紀錄片	so we showed the documentary film there .
一週之後他們組織了一場在當時參與人數最多最有紀律的遊行示威	a week later , they organized the most disciplined protest to participate at the time .
組織者們說當村民在紀錄片中看到佈德魯斯的故事他們感覺到確實有人與他們志同道合人們是在乎的	the organizers said that when the villagers saw bedrus in his documentary film , they felt that there was a real sense that people really cared with them .
於是他們沒有放棄	so they didn't give up .
以色列有一個新的和平運動被稱為 " 索裡德拉爾特 " 在希伯來語中意為 " 團結一致 "	israel has a new peace movement called soledret , which means " unity " in the hebrew language .
佈德魯斯的故事成為了這個運動的領導者招兵買馬的主要手段之一	and broadruce's story became one of the leaders of the movement to recruit himself to buy horses .
他們反映說那些從未加入任何運動的以色列人看了紀錄片之後瞭解了非暴力抵抗的力量並開始加入他們行動	they reflected that israelis who had never joined any movement had seen documentaries and understood the power of nonviolent resistance and began to join them .
瓦拉傑和索裡德拉爾特運動的例子告訴我們即使是小成本的獨立電影也能夠幫助非暴力抵抗轉變為一種功能性行為	the varaje and solid laurate movements have shown us that even small independent films can help nonviolent resistance to be functional .
想象一下主流媒體若是開始報道每週在貝拉因尼亞林瓦拉傑等村莊以及耶路撒冷境內的香克哈拉和西路萬巴勒斯坦居住區裡發生的非暴力示威活動這將產生多麼巨大的力量更多的人會關注非暴力運動領導者重視他們讓他們的工作更有成效	imagine if mainstream media started reporting about villages like bellau lynwaraj , and choke harala in jerusalem , and the nonviolent demonstrations in the habitat residence of the palestinian neighborhood , which is so enormous that more people pay attention to nonviolent activists and make their work better .
我相信最重要的是我們要認識到如果我們不關注這些運動它們就是隱形的彷彿從來沒有發生過	i believe the most important thing to recognize is that if we don't pay attention to these movements , they are invisible as if they haven't happened before .
但我以親身經歷為證如果我們關注這些運動就會得到發展	but i testify as a personal experience that if we pay attention to these movements , we'll be developed .
它們一旦發展其影響力就會遍及巴以衝突	when they develop their influence , they're all over the palestinian conflict .
這種影響能夠最終將衝突化解	this influence ultimately resolves conflict .
這些領導者證明了非暴力運動在佈德魯斯這樣的地方是可行的	these leaders proved that nonviolent movements work in places like dress .
我們一起來關注他們讓他們證明這在任何地方都是可行的	and we watched them , and they showed that it was possible anywhere .
西蒙•斯涅克用一個簡單但是震撼的模型來闡釋激勵人心的領袖力 , 這個模型的核心是一個 " 黃金 " 圓圈 , 意思是領袖素質的根本來源是回答 " 為什麼 ? " 。 他列舉了蘋果公司、馬丁•路德•金還有萊特兄弟成功的例子 , 同時以蒂沃數碼錄影機為失敗的典型 。 雖然蒂沃最近打贏一場官司 , 使得其股價上漲了3倍 , 但是它仍在掙扎中 。	simone snoneck illustrates the inspirational leadership in the heart of this model , which is a golden circle , meaning the fundamental source of the leader's quality is " why ? " he lists apple , martin luther king and wright's brother's successful example , and loses the typical digital video clip .
bullseye , business , entrepreneur , leadership , sales , selling , success	bull seye , it's a state of entrepreneur , it's no longer true , it's sales , selling , it's success .
西蒙•斯涅克:偉大的領袖如何激勵行動	simone snonek: how great leaders inspire action .
當事情的發展出乎意料之外的時候 , 你怎麼解釋 ?	how do you explain when things are developing unexpectedly ?
換句話說 , 當別人似乎出乎意料地取得成功的時候 , 你怎麼解釋 ?	in other words , how do you explain when someone seems to be successful in unexpected ways ?
比如說 , 為什麼蘋果公司創新能力這麼強 ?	for example , why is apple so innovative ?
這麼多年來 , 年復一年 , 他們比所有競爭對手都更加具有創新性 。	over the years , years and years , they've been more innovative than all their competition .
而其實他們只是一家電腦公司 。	and they're actually just a computer company .
他們跟其他公司沒有任何分別 ,	they didn't have anything to do with the other companies .
有同樣的途徑 , 接觸到同樣的人才 , 同樣的代理商 , 顧問 , 和媒體 。	there are the same pathways , exposure to the same talents , the same agents , the consultants , the media .
那為什麼他們就似乎有那麼一點不同尋常呢 ?	so why do they seem to be so remarkable ?
同樣的 , 為什麼是由馬丁•路德•金來領導民權運動 ?	similarly , why is it that martin luther king came to lead the civil rights movement ?
那個時候在美國 , 民權運動之前 , 不僅僅只有他一個人飽受歧視 。 他也決不是那個時代唯一的偉大演說家 。	at that time , before the civil rights movement , it wasn't just himself suffering discrimination , it was determined that he was not the only great orator of the time .
又為什麼懷特兄弟能夠造出動力控制的載人飛機 , 跟他們相比 , 當時的其他團隊似乎更有能力 , 更有資金 ,	and why the white brothers were able to create drivers who were able to control , compared to them , other teams at the time seemed more capable , more funded .
他們卻沒能製造出載人飛機 , 懷特兄弟打敗了他們 。	they didn't make a carrier airplane , and the white brothers beat them .
一定還有一些什麼別的因素在起作用 。	there must be some other factors that are going on .
大概三年半之前 , 我有了個新發現 ,	about three and a half years ago , i made a new discovery .
這個發現完全改變了我對這個世界如何運作的看法 。 甚至從根本上改變了我的工作生活方式 。	this discovery completely changed how i think about how the world works , and even fundamentally changed the way i work .
那就是我發現了一種模式 ,	and that's how i discovered a pattern .
我發現世界上所有偉大的令人振奮的領袖和組織 , 無論是蘋果公司、馬丁•路德•金還是懷特兄弟 , 他們思考、行動、交流溝通的方式都完全一樣 ,	i find out that all the great leaders and organizations in the world , whether it's apple or martin luther king or white brothers , they think , act , communicate in exactly the same way .
但是跟所有其他人的方式完全相反 。	but the opposite is true of everybody else .
我所做的僅僅是把它整理出來 。 這可能是世上最簡單的概念 。	all i did was to organize it . it's probably the simplest concept in the world .
我稱它為黃金圓環 。	i call it the golden circle .
為什麼 ? 怎麼做 ? 是什麼 ?	why ? how ? what ?
這小小的模型就解釋了為什麼一些組織和領導者能夠在別人不能的地方激發出靈感和潛力 。	this little model explains why some organizations and leaders can inspire and potential where others cannot .
我來儘快地解釋一下這些術語 。	i'm going to explain those terms very quickly .
地球上的每個人 , 每個組織都明白自己做的是什麼 , 百分之百 。	everyone on this planet , every organization on this planet , understood what they were doing , 100 percent .
其中一些知道該怎麼做 , 你可以稱之為是你的差異價值 , 或是你的獨特工藝 , 或是你的獨特賣點也好 , 怎麼說都行 。	some of them know what to do , and you can call it your differences , or your unique craft , or your unique tradeoffs , or your unique sales point , or whatever .
但是非常 , 非常少的人和組織明白為什麼做 。	but very , very few people and organizations understand why .
這裡的 " 為什麼 " 和 " 為利潤 " 沒有關係 ,	there's nothing to do with " why " and " profit " here .
利潤只是一個結果 , 永遠只能是一個結果 。	profits are just one result , always one result .
我說的 " 為什麼 " 指的是:你的目的是什麼 ?	and by " why " i mean: what is your purpose ?
你這樣做的原因是什麼 ? 你懷著什麼樣的信念 ?	what's the reason you do that ? what kind of beliefs do you hold ?
你的機構為什麼而存在 ?	why does your organization exist ?
你每天早上是為什麼而起床 ?	why did you get up every morning ?
為什麼別人要在乎你 ?	why should anyone care ?
結果是 , 我們思考的方式 , 行動的方式 , 交流的方式都是由外向內的 。	and it turns out that the way we think , the way we move , the way we communicate , is both extroverted .
很顯然的 , 我們所採用的方式是從清晰開始 , 然後到模糊的東西 。	clearly , what we're doing is starting with clarity , and then blurry stuff .
但是激勵型領袖以及組織機構 , 無論他們的規模大小 , 所在領域 , 他們思考 , 行動和交流的方式都是從裡向外的 。	but inspiration leaders and organizations , no matter what size they are , they think , move and communicate from the inside out .
舉個例子吧 。	let's take an example .
我舉蘋果公司是因為這個例子簡單易懂 , 每個人都能理解 。	i'll give you an apple because it's easy to understand , everybody understands it .
如果蘋果公司跟其他公司一樣 , 他們的市場營銷資訊就會是這個樣子: " 我們做最棒的電腦 ,	if apple was like any other company , this is what marketing information would look like: " we make the best computers .
設計精美 , 使用簡單 , 介面友好 。	design beautiful , using simple , interface friendly .
你想買一臺嗎 ? " 不怎麼樣吧 。	do you want to buy one ? "
這就是我們大多數人的交流方式 ,	this is how most of us communicate .
也是大多數市場推廣的方式 , 大部分銷售所採用的方式 , 也是我們大部分人互相交流的方式 。	and that's how most markets push , most sales adopt , and how most of us interact with each other .
我們說我們的職業是幹什麼的 , 我們說我們是如何的與眾不同 , 或者我們怎麼比其他人更好 , 然後我們就期待著一些別人的反應 , 比如購買 , 比如投票 , 諸如此類 。	we say what our profession does , we say how we're different or how we're better than others , and then we expect other people to respond , like purchasing , like voting , and so on .
這是我們新開的的律師事務所 , 我們擁有最棒的律師和最大的客戶 , 我們總是能滿足客戶的要求 。	this is our newly open law firm , and we have the best lawyers and the biggest customers , and we can always fulfill our clients' needs .
這是我們的新車型 , 非常省油 , 真皮座椅 。 買一輛吧 。	this is our new carshaped , very fuelefficient , dermis . buy one .
這是蘋果公司實際上的溝通方式:	this is how apple actually communicates .
" 我們做的每一件事情 , 都是為了突破和創新 。	" everything we do for breakthroughs and innovation .
我們堅信應該以不同的方式思考 。	we firmly believe that we should think differently .
我們挑戰現狀的方式是透過把我們的產品設計得十分精美 , 使用簡單 , 和介面友好 。	the way we challenge the status quo is by designing our products beautifully , using simplicity and interface friendship .
我們只是在這個過程中做出了最棒的電腦 。	we just made the best computer in the process .
想買一臺嗎 ? "	would you like to buy one ? "
感覺完全不一樣 , 對吧 ? 你已經準備從我這裡買一臺了 。	it feels completely different , right ? you're ready to buy from me .
我所做的只是將傳遞資訊的順序顛倒一下而已 。	all i did was to reverse the order of the information transmitted .
事實已經向我們證明 , 人們買的不是你做的產品 , 人們買的是你的信念和宗旨 。	as it turns out , people are not buying products that you do , people are buying your beliefs and missions .
人們買的不是你做的產品 , 人們買的是你的信念 。	people don't buy your products ; people buy your beliefs .
這就解釋了為什麼這裡的每個人從蘋果公司買電腦時都覺得理所當然 。	this explains why everyone here takes it for granted when they buy a computer from an apple .
但是我們從蘋果公司買mp3播放器 , 手機 , 或者數碼攝像機時 , 也感覺很舒服 。	but when we bought an mp3 player from an apple , a cell phone , or a digital camera , it felt very comfortable .
而其實 , 我剛才已經說過 , 蘋果公司只是個電腦公司 。	and actually , as i said earlier , apple is just a computer company .
沒有什麼能從結構上將蘋果公司同競爭對手區分開來 。	there's nothing structural that separates the apple from the competition .
競爭對手和蘋果公司有同樣的能力製造所有這些產品 。	competitors have the same capacity as apple to make all of these products .
實際上 , 他們也嘗試過 。	in fact , they tried .
幾年前 , 捷威公司推出了平板電視 。	a few years ago , the czech company introduced a flatscreen tv .
他們製造平板電視的能力很強 ,	they're very capable of making tablets .
因為他們做平板顯示器已經很多年了 。	because they've been working on a tablet display for years .
戴爾公司推出了mp3播放器和掌上電腦 , 他們產品的質量非常好 , 產品的設計也非常不錯 。 但是也沒有人買他們的這些產品 。	and darre launched an mp3 player and a palmpilot , whose product was very good , and the product was designed very well , but nobody bought them .
其實 , 說到這裡 , 我們無法想象會從戴爾公司買mp3播放器 。	actually , when it comes to this , we can't imagine buying an mp3 player from dell .
你為什麼會從一家電腦公司買mp3播放器呢 ?	why would you buy an mp3 player from a computer company ?
但是每天我們都這麼做 。	but we do it every day .
人們買的不是你做的產品 , 人們買的是你的信念 。	people don't buy your products ; people buy your beliefs .
做公司的目標不是要跟所有需要你的產品的人做生意 ,	the goal of the company is not to do business with everybody who needs your product .
而是跟與你有著相同理念的人做生意 。	it's a business with people who have the same ideas .
這是最精彩的部分 。 我說的這些沒有一個是我自己的觀點 。	that's the best part . none of those i'm talking about are my own perspective .
這些觀點都能從生物學裡面找到根源 。	all of these views can be found in biology .
不是心理學 , 是生物學 。	not psychology , but biology .
當你俯視看大腦的橫截面 , 你會發現人類大腦實際上分成三個主要部分 , 而這三個主要部分和黃金圓環匹配得非常好 。	when you look at the crossection of the brain , you can see that the human brain is actually split into three key parts , and these three main components are very good at matching the golden circle .
我們最新的腦部 , 管轄智力的腦部 , 或者說我們的大腦皮層 , 對應著 " 是什麼 " 這個圓環 。	our latest brain , the jurisdictional brain , or our cerebral cortex , corresponds to this circle .
大腦皮層負責我們所有的理性和邏輯的思考和語言功能 。	the cortex is responsible for all of our rational and logical thinking and language function .
中間的兩個部分是我們的兩個邊腦 。 邊腦負責我們所有的情感 , 比如信任和忠誠 ,	the two parts in the middle are our brains , and the brain is responsible for all of our emotions , like trust and loyalty .
也負責所有的行為和決策 , 但這部分沒有語言功能 。	it's also responsible for all behaviors and decisions , but this part doesn't have any linguistic function .
換句話說 , 當我們由外向內交流時 , 沒錯 , 人們可以理解大量的複雜資訊 , 比如特徵 , 優點 , 事實和圖表 。	in other words , when we communicate inwardly , yes , people can understand a lot of complex information , like features , strength , facts and graphs .
但不足以激發行動 。	but it's not enough to activate .
當我們由內向外交流時 , 我們是在直接同控制行為的那一部分大腦對話 , 然後我們由人們理性地思考我們所說和做的事情 。	when we're diplomacying diplomacy , we're directly controlling behavior , and then we're rationally thinking about what we're saying and doing .
這就是那些發自內心的決定的來源 。	that's where those decisions come from .
你知道 , 有時候你展示給一些人所有的資料圖表 , 他們會說 " 我知道這些資料和圖表是什麼意思 , 但就是感覺不對 。 "	you know , sometimes you show people all the data graphs , and they say , " i know what these data and graphs mean , but it just doesn't feel right . "
為什麼我們會用這個動詞 , " 感覺 " 不對 ?	why do we use that verb , " feeling " ?
因為控制決策的那一部分大腦並不支配語言 ,	because the part of the brain that controls decisionmaking doesn't govern language .
我們只好說 " 我不知道為什麼 , 就是感覺不對 。 "	we just said , " i don't know why , it just feels wrong . "
或者有些時候 , 你說聽從心的召喚 , 或者說聽從靈魂 。	or sometimes you hear the call , or you hear from the heart , or from the soul .
我不想把這些觀念分解得太徹底 , 但心和靈魂都不是控制行為的部分 。	i don't want to break these ideas down too thoroughly , but the heart and the soul are not the parts that control behavior .
所有這一切都發生在你的邊腦 , 控制決策行為而非語言的邊腦 。	all of this happens in your brain to control decisionmaking behavior rather than linguistic brains .
如果你自己都不知道你為什麼幹你所做的事情 , 而別人要對你的動機作出反應 , 那麼你怎麼可能贏得大家對你的支援 , 從你這裡購買東西 , 或者 , 更重要的 , 對你忠誠並且想成為你正在做的事情的一分子呢 ?	if you don't know why you're doing what you're doing , and people are responding to your motivations , then how can you win people's support from you , buying things from you , or , more importantly , loyal to you and wanting to be part of what you're doing ?
再說一次 , 目標不僅僅是將你有的東西賣給需要它們的人 ; 而是將東西賣給跟你有共同信念的人 。	and again , the goal is not just to sell the things you have to people who need them ; it's to sell them to people who share your beliefs .
目標不僅僅是僱傭那些需要一份工作的人 ; 目標是僱傭那些同你有共同信念的人 。	the goal is not just to employ those who need a job ; the goal is to employ those who share a common belief .
你知道嗎 , 我總是說 , 如果你僱傭某人只是因為他能做這份工作 , 他們就只是為你開的工資而工作 , 但是如果你僱傭跟你有共同信念的人 , 他們會為你付出熱血 , 汗水和淚水 。	you know , i always say , if you hire someone just because they can do this work , they're just working for you salary , but if you employ someone with you , they will pay you blood , sweat and tears .
這一點 , 沒有比懷特兄弟的故事更恰當的例子了 。	now , no more appropriate example than the white brothers' stories .
大多數人都沒聽說過塞繆爾•蘭利這個人 。	most of you have never heard of samuel lanley .
20世紀初期 , 投入機動飛行器的熱情就像當今的網站熱 ,	in the early 20th century , the passion to invest in motorized robots was like the current website .
每個人都在做嘗試 。	everybody was trying .
塞繆爾•蘭利擁有所有大家認為是成功的要素 。	samuel landley had all the elements of success .
我的意思是 , 即便是現在 , 你問別人 " 為什麼你的產品或者公司失敗了呢 ? "	i mean , even now , you ask people , " why did your product or your company fail ? "
人們總是用同樣的三個東西以同樣的排列順序來回答你 , 缺乏資金 , 用人不善 , 形勢不好 。	people are always answering you with the same three things in the same order: lack of funding , poor people , bad posture .
總是那三種理由 , 所以讓我們來逐個分析一下 。	those are the three reasons , so let's go through one analysis .
國防部給了塞繆爾•蘭利5萬美金作為研製飛行器的資金 。	the department of defense funded samuel lanlee 50 , 000 dollars as a robot .
所以說 , 資金不是問題 。	so funding is not a problem .
他在哈佛大學工作過 , 也在史密森尼學會工作過 , 人脈極其廣泛 。 他認識當時最優秀的人才 。	he worked at harvard university , and he worked at the smithsonian society , incredibly wide , and he knew the best people at the time .
因此 , 他僱傭了用資金能吸引到的最優秀的人才 。 當時的市場形勢相當有利 。	so he hired domesticated talent with the best people he could attract , which was a very good market condition .
紐約時報對他做跟蹤報道 , 每個人都支援他 。	the new york times reported to him , and everyone supported him .
但是為什麼你們連聽都沒聽說過他呢 ?	but why have you not even heard of him ?
與此同時 , 幾百公里之外的俄亥俄州代頓市有一對兄弟 , 奧維爾•萊特和維爾伯•萊特 , 他們倆沒有任何我們認為的成功的要素 。	meanwhile , hundreds of kilometers away in submitton , ohio , orville wright and virgin wright , they didn't have any elements for success .
他們沒有錢 。 他們用腳踏車店的收入來追求他們的夢想 。 萊特兄弟的團隊中沒有一個人上過大學 , 就連奧維爾和維爾伯也沒有 。 紐約時報更是不沾邊的 。	they didn't have money . they were pursuing their dreams with income in a bicycle shop , and none of the teams in the wright brothers had gone to college , even ovial and virgin , and the new york times were more impressive .
不同的是 , 奧維爾和維爾伯追求的是一個事業 , 一個目標 , 一種信念 。	what's different is that orville and velber are pursuing a career , a goal , a belief .
他們相信如果他們能研製出飛行器 , 將會改變全世界的發展程序 。	they believe that if they could build a robot , they would change the course of development worldwide .
塞繆爾•蘭利就不同了 ,	samuel landley was different .
他想要發財 , 他想要成名 。	he wanted to finance , he wanted to be famous .
他追求的是最終結果 ,	he was looking for the end result .
是變得富有 。	it's becoming rich .
看吧 , 看接下來怎麼樣了 。	see , look what happened .
那些懷有和懷特兄弟一樣夢想的人跟他們一起熱血朝天地奮鬥著 。	those who had the same dreams as the white brothers struggled with them towards the heavens .
另一邊的人則是為了工資而工作 。	on the other side , people work for salary .
後來流傳的故事說 , 每次懷特兄弟出去實驗時 , 都必須帶著五組零件 , 因為那是在他們回來吃晚飯之前將要墜毀的次數 。	and the stories that came later said that every time the white brothers went out to experiment , they had to carry five pieces , because that was the number of times they were about to crash before they came back for dinner .
最後 , 在1903年12月17日 , 懷特兄弟成功起飛 , 但是當時沒有任何其他人在場目睹 。	finally , on december 17 , 1903 , the white brothers took off , but nobody else was there .
我們是在幾天後才知道的 。	we didn't know that until a few days later .
後來的事情進一步證實了蘭利動機不純 , 他在懷特兄弟成功的當天就辭職了 。	and then something happened further confirmed that the langley motivation was innocent , and he quit his job on the day of the white brothers .
他本來應該可以說: " 夥計們 , 這真是一項偉大的發明 , 我可以改進你們的技術 。 " 但是他沒有 ,	he was supposed to be able to say , " guys , this is a great invention , and i can improve your technology . "
因為他不是第一個製造出飛機的人 , 他就不會變得富有 , 他也不會變得有名 , 所以他辭職了 。	because he wasn't the first person to make an airplane , he wouldn't be rich , and he wouldn't be famous , so he quit .
人們買的不是你的產品 ; 而是你的信念 。	people are not buying your product ; they're your beliefs .
如果你講述你的信念 , 你將吸引那些跟你擁有同樣信念的人 。	if you talk about your beliefs , you will attract people who share your beliefs .
但是為什麼吸引那些跟你擁有同樣信念的人非常重要呢 ?	but why is it so important to attract people who share the same beliefs ?
創新的傳播有一個規律 , 如果你不知道這個規律 , 你一定了解這個概念 。	there's a pattern innovation spreading , and if you don't know the pattern , you get this idea .
我們的社會中 , 有2.5%的人是革新者 。	2 . 5 percent of our society is innovators .
13.5%的人是早期的少部分採納者 。	thirty . 5 percent of people were early adopters .
接下來的34%是早期接受的大多數 , 然後是比較晚接受的大多數和最後行動的 。	the next 34 percent is early acceptance , then most and final action later .
這部分最後行動的人買按鍵電話的唯一原因是因為他們再也買不到轉盤電話了 。	the only reason these guys ended up buying a phone call is because they couldn't buy a cell phone anymore .
雖然我們在不同的時候會處在這個曲線上不同的位置 , 但是創新的傳播規律告訴我們如果你想在大眾市場上獲得成功 , 或者要大眾接納一個點子 , 你得等到獲得15%-18%的市場接受度這個轉折點之後才行 。 那時之後市場才真正開啟 。	although we're different at different times on this curve , the innovation pattern of communication tells us that if you want to succeed in massmarket success or accept an idea for the public , you have to wait until you get 15 to 18 percent of the market reception points , and that's when the market really opens .
我喜歡問公司: " 你的新生意怎麼樣呀 ? "	i like to ask companies , " what's your business ? "
他們會很自豪地告訴你 " 哦 , 大概有10%吧 。 "	they'll be proud to tell you , " oh , about 10 percent . "
是呀 , 你有可能就在10%的顧客群這裡過不去了 。	yeah , you're likely to be here in 10 percent of customers .
我們都能讓10%的人 " 意會 " ,	we can all get 10 percent of the people .
對 , 我們一般這樣形容他們 。	yeah , we typically describe them .
就好比描述那種感覺: " 哦 , 他們有點心領神會了 " 。	it's like describing that feeling , " oh , they're a little bit gutwrenched . "
問題是:你怎麼在他們還沒有成為你的顧客之前就發現那些能意會的人 , 和那些不能意會的人 ?	the question is: how did you find people who could not agree before they were your customers ?
這就是問題的所在 , 就是這點間隙 , 你得把這個間隙給填上 , 正如傑弗裡穆爾所說的 , " 跨越鴻溝 " 。 因為早期的大多數不會嘗試新事物 , 除非有些人已經先嚐試過了 。	that's the problem , and that's the point where you have to fill this gap , as jeffrey moore said , " cross the gap , " because the early majority won't try something new unless some people have tried it first .
而這些人 , 創新者和早期的少數人 , 他們喜歡大膽的嘗試 。	and these guys , the innovators and the early few , they like the bold try .
他們更自然地憑直覺做事情 , 發自於他們的世界觀的直覺 , 而不僅僅是因為市場上有什麼樣的產品 。	they naturally do things intuitively , instinctively from their worldviews , not just because of the products on the market .
這是一批在iphone上市的頭幾天去排隊等六個小時來購買的人 , 而其實只要等一個星期你就可以隨便走進店裡從貨架上買到 。	this was the first time a iphone came in line to wait six hours to buy it , and in fact , waiting for a week to go to the store and buy it from the shelves .
這是一批在平板電視剛推出時會花4萬美金買一臺的人 , 儘管當時的技術還不成熟 。	this was a batch of people who spent 40 , 000 dollars on a flatscreen television , although the technologies were not mature at the time .
補充說一下 , 他們並不是因為技術的先進而買那些產品 , 而是為了他們自己 。	in addition , they're not buying those products because of technological advancement , but for themselves .
因為他們想成為第一個體驗新產品的人 。	because they want to be the first person to experience a new product .
人們買的不是你的產品 ; 人們買的是你的信念 。 你的行動只是證明了你的信念 。	people didn't buy your product ; people bought your beliefs ; your actions proved your beliefs .
實際上 , 人們會去做能夠體現他們的信念的事情 。	in fact , people do things that embody their beliefs .
那些為了搶先在頭六個小時內買到iphone而排六個小時的隊的人 , 是出於他們的世界觀 , 出於他們想別人怎麼看自己 。 他們是第一批體驗者 。	the people who bought an iphone six hours in the first six hours were their worldviews , out of what they wanted other people to see themselves . they were the first subjects .
人們買的不是你的產品 ; 他們買的是你的信念 。	people don't buy your product ; they buy your beliefs .
我再舉些著名的例子吧 , 證實創新傳播規律的一個失敗的例子和一個成功的例子 。	let me give you some more famous examples of the failure of innovation in spreading patterns and a successful example .
首先我們講這個失敗的例子 。	let's start with this failure .
還是商業上的 。	it's a business .
就如我們一秒鐘前剛剛說過的 , 成功的要素是充足的資金 , 優秀的人才和良好的市場形勢 。 那麼 , 是不是如果有這些你就應該獲得成功 。	as we said just a second ago , the element of success is financial , great talent and good markets . so , if you have those , you should be successful .
自從推出蒂沃機頂盒以來 , 大概是八、九年前 , 直到今天 , 它們一直是市場上唯一的最高品質的產品 , 這沒有任何異議 。	it's been about eight or nine years ago since the roofbox launched , until today , they've been the only highest quality product on the market , and there's no difference .
它們絕對是資金充足 ,	they're absolutely sufficient .
市場形勢也大好 。	markets are great .
其實 , " 蒂沃 " 都變成了一個日常用的動詞 。	in fact , " tive " became a daily verb .
比如:我經常把東西蒂沃到我那臺華納數碼影片錄影機裡面 。	for instance , i often get things tiwalwood in my warner digital video camera .
但是蒂沃是個商業上的失敗案例 ,	but tivel was a failure in business .
他們沒有賺到一分錢 。	they didn't make a penny .
他們上市時 , 股票價格大約在30到40美元 , 然後就直線下跌 , 而成交價格從沒超過10美元 。	when they came out , the price of the stock was between 30 and 40 dollars , and then it went straight down , and the cost was never over 10 dollars .
實際上 , 我印象中它的交易價格從來沒有超過6美元 , 除了幾次小的震盪之外 。	in fact , i remember its price for trade was never over six dollars , except a few tiny concussions .
因為你會發現 , 蒂沃公司新推出他們的產品時 , 他們只是告訴我們他們產品是什麼 ,	because you'll notice that when tiwo launched their product , they just told us what their product was .
他們說 " 我們的產品可以把電視節目暫停 , 跳過廣告 , 回放電視節目 , 還能記住你的觀看習慣 , 你甚至都不用刻意設定它 。 "	they said , " our products can pause the television program , skip ads , release television programs , and remember your habits , and you don't even have to set it intentionally . "
挑剔的人們說: " 我們不相信你 ,	critical people say , " we don't trust you .
我們不需要這樣的東西 , 我們也不喜歡這樣的東西 。	we don't need something like this , and we don't like that either .
你在唬人 。 "	you're bluffing people . "
假如他們這麼說: " 如果你想掌控生活的方方面面 , 朋友 , 那麼就試試我們的產品吧 。	if they say , " if you want to take control of the aspects of life , friends , try our product .
它可以暫停直播節目 , 跳過廣告 , 回放直播節目 , 還能記下你的觀看習慣 , 等等 。	it pauses livestreaming , skips advertising , releases livestreaming , and remembers your watching habits , etc .
人們買的不是你的產品 ; 人們買的是你的信念 。 你所做的僅僅只是你的信念的證明而已 。	people don't buy your product ; people buy your beliefs .
下面我給大家介紹一個成功的例子 。	i'm going to show you a successful example .
1963年的夏天 , 25萬人聚集在華盛頓特區聆聽馬丁•路德•金博士的演講 。	in the summer of 1963 , 250 , 000 people gathered in washington , d . c . to listen to dr . martin luther king speak .
那時 , 既沒有發請帖 , 也沒有可能在網上檢視日期 。	there was no review , no possibility of looking at the date online .
怎麼會有25萬人參加呢 ?	how do you get 250 , 000 people involved ?
而且 , 金博士不是美國唯一的偉大演說家 ,	and dr . king wasn't the only great american orator .
也不是美國唯一一位在民權法案實施前遭受歧視的人 。	it's not the only person in the united states who suffered discrimination before the civil rights act .
實際上 , 他的一些想法甚至不正確 。	in fact , some of his ideas weren't even right .
但是他有個天賦 。	but he had a gift .
他沒有到處宣揚美國需要改變什麼方面 ,	he didn't go around saying what the united states needed to change .
他只是到處告訴別人他所相信的 。	he was just telling people what he believed .
" 我相信 。 我相信 。 我相信 。 " 他總是這麼跟別人說 。	" i believe . i believe . " he said to people all the time .
而那些和他懷有同樣信念的人受了他的啟發 , 他們也開始將自己的信念告訴別人 。	and he was inspired by those who had the same beliefs , and they began to tell people about their beliefs .
有些人建立起一些組織機構將這些話傳給更多的人 。	there are people who are building organizations that are sending these to more people .
你看 , 就這樣 , 25萬人在那天 , 那個時候 , 聚集在一起聽他演講 。	you see , 250 , 000 people were there that day , when he got together and heard him speak .
有多少人是為了聽 " 他 " 演說而去的呢 ?	how many people did it for " he " ?
他們是為了他們自己而去的 。	they were there for themselves .
那是他們對於美國的信念支援著他們坐8個小時的公車 , 站在華盛頓八月中旬的烈日下 。	it was their faith in the united states supporting them by sitting eight hours on the bus day of washington in the middle of august .
是他們所相信的信念 , 而不是黑人跟白人之間的鬥爭 。 25%的聽眾是白人 。	it's the belief that they believe , not the struggle between black and white , 25 percent of the audience is white .
金博士相信世界上有兩種律法 , 一種是上天制定的 , 一種是世人制定的 。	dr . king believed there were two laws in the world , one that were made up in the world , one that was made up of the world .
直到世人制定的法律和上天制定的律法相符合 , 我們才真正生活在公正的世界裡 。	it wasn't until the laws that made up of the world meet the laws that made up of the day that we really live in a world of justice .
民權運動只是碰巧幫他將信念付諸於現實的一件事情 。	the civil rights movement just happened to help him fix his beliefs on reality .
我們跟隨他 , 不是為了他 , 而是為了我們自己 。	we followed him , not for him , but for ourselves .
順便說一下 , 他的演講是 " 我有一個夢想 " , 而不是 " 我有一個方案 " 。	by the way , his talk is " i have a dream " speech , not " i have a solution . "
聽聽現在的政治家們提出的12點的大雜燴計劃 ,	listen to the 12point politicians that are proposing .
沒一點勁 。	nothing .
一些人是當官的 , 而另一些人是領袖 。	some people are official , and others are leaders .
當官的只是佔據在有權力和威嚴的位置上 , 但是隻有具有領袖素質的人才能激勵我們 。	they are occupying the position of power and strictness , but a person with leadership quality can inspire us .
無論他們是個人還是組織 , 我們都追隨領袖 , 不是因為我們必須這樣做 , 而是因為我們願意 。	whether they're individuals or organizations , we follow leaders , not because we have to do it , but because we want to .
我們跟隨具有領袖能力的人 , 不是為他們 , 而是為我們自己 。	we follow people with leadership , not for them , but for ourselves .
也只有那些從 " 為什麼 " 這個圓圈出發的人才有能力激勵周圍的人 , 或者找到能夠激勵他們的人 。	it's the people who come from the " why " circle who have the ability to motivate surroundings , or find the people who can motivate them .
你是如何回憶起將車停在了什麼地方呢 ? 你怎麼判斷自己是否走對了方向呢 ? 神經系統科學家尼爾•伯吉斯研究了神經系統的定位功能原理 , 以及該原理與記憶和想象的關係 。	how did you recall where you parked your car , and how did you judge whether you were in the right direction , the neuroscientist neil bergius studied the functionality of the nervous system and the relationship between the principle and the memory and the imagination ?
brain , cognitivescience , exploration , neuroscience , science	this is cognitivescience .
尼爾•伯吉斯:大腦是怎樣幫我們定位的	nels boggius: how does the brain work for us ?
當我們在大型停車場停車後 , 如何回憶起將車停在了哪個車位呢 ?	how do we recall where we parked our car after a large parking lot ?
這就是現在困擾荷馬的問題 。	that's the problem with homer .
接下來我們將嘗試瞭解此時他腦中正開展何種 " 運動 " 。	and then we're going to try to figure out what kind of exercise is going on in his head right now .
我們先著眼於大腦海馬區 , 即黃色的區域這是我們的記憶器官 。	we started by looking at the hippocampus , the yellow area this is our memory organ .
如果海馬區出現損傷 , 像老年痴呆症患者一樣 , 你將喪失記憶力 , 乃至記不起將車停在了何處 。	if there's a damage to the hippocampus , like an alzheimer's patient , you can't remember where the car is going .
hippocampus這個詞源自拉丁語 , 有 " 海馬 " 之意因為腦中海馬區的形狀看上去有點像 " 海馬 " 。	the hippocampus comes from latin , which means " hippocampus " because the shape of the hippocampus looks a little bit like " hippocampus . "
海馬區和大腦其它區域的組成相似 , 都由神經元構成 。	the hippocampus is similar to the rest of the brain , made of neurons .
人的大腦由大約一千億個神經元細胞組成 。	the human brain is made up of about 100 billion neurons .
每個神經元細胞之間透過一些連線中介互相傳送小的電脈衝或者尖峰電壓來進行 " 交流 " 。	each of these neurons communicates through some of the connections between these neurons , or peak communication .
海馬區由兩層片狀的細胞群構成 , 這兩層細胞群緊密相連 。	the hippocampus is made up of two layers of cells that are intimately connected .
科學家們透過記錄老鼠在某環境中搜羅食物時其腦中單個神經元細胞的反應來了解 " 空間記憶 " 的工作原理與工作機制 。	scientists understand the response to spatial memory and the work mechanisms of spatial memory in a given environment .
現在想象一下 , 我們正在為這隻老鼠的海馬區中的一個神經元細胞 " 錄影 " 。	now imagine that we're recording a neuron in the hippocampus of this mouse .
每當這個細胞發出小型尖峰電壓 , 隨後會出現一個紅點以及咔噠的一聲 。	every time this cell sends a small peak peak pressure , there's a red dot and a click sound .
我們可以看出每當老鼠進入環境中某一特定位置 , 這個神經元細胞便會有反應 。	we can see that every time a mouse enters a certain location in the environment , this neuron will respond .
然後這個細胞再透過小型尖峰電壓將以上資訊傳遞給大腦的其它區域 。	and this cell then sends information to other parts of the brain through a small peak .
這麼一來 , 我們可以憑藉這個細胞傳送訊號的頻率推知老鼠經過的相應位置 。	in this way , we can tell where the rat goes by by by by the frequency of the cell .
倘若我們記錄的是很多不同的神經元細胞 , 就會發現當老鼠處於不同的位置上時 , 不同的神經元細胞會產生各自的電訊號 , 正如我們在這些方形中看到的那樣 。	if we document a lot of different neurons , we find that different neurons produce their own electrical signals as we see them in different locations .
這些訊號為大腦中的其它區域勾勒出一張地圖 , 持續地向大腦指示出 , " 我現在位於環境中的哪個具體點上 ? "	these signals are mapped in other parts of the brain , constantly instructing to the brain , " what specific point am i in the environment right now ? "
我們也記錄人腦中的 " 定位神經元細胞 " 。	we also document " location neurons " in the human brain .
癲癇病患者有時需要監測他們的腦電活動情況 。	patients with epilepsy sometimes need to monitor their brain electrical activity .
一些患者玩一種電子遊戲 , 遊戲中他們在一個小鎮上自由開車 。	some patients played a video game where they were free to drive in a small town .
然後當他們驅車駛過鎮上的某一處時 , 他們大腦海馬區中的 " 定位神經元細胞 " 便會被啟用 , 發出訊號 。	and then when they're driving somewhere in town , their location neuron in the hippocampus will be inspired , sending out signals .
那麼這 " 定位細胞 " 是怎麼知道老鼠或人處於某個位置的呢 ?	so how does this position cell know that mice or people are somewhere ?
這裡有兩個神經元細胞 , 它們告訴我們 , 在定位時環境的邊界是至關重要的 。	here are two neurons , and they tell us that the boundaries in a positioning environment are essential .
上面的這個細胞傾向於在老鼠向盒子中部走去時產生訊號 。	this cell up there tends to produce a signal as it travels in the middle of the box .
因此當你將盒子擴大 , 相應的訊號活躍區也隨之擴大 。	so when you expand the box , the signal activity zone expands .
下面的這個喜歡在老鼠緊鄰南面屏障時作出反應 。	this one underneath the mouse responds to a southern barrier .
因此當你在盒中放入另一屏障時 , 不論老鼠在盒中何處 , 只要它的南面有屏障 , 該細胞中的相應位置便會同時產生訊號 。	so when you put another barrier in the box , wherever the mouse is in the box , if it has a screen in the south , the correspondence in that cell will be produced at the same time .
這表明瞭解到達邊界比如周邊的建築物等需要的距離和方向對於海馬區的 " 工作 " 而言至關重要 。	it's indicating that the distance and direction that's necessary to reach the border of buildings like the one around the hippocampus is essential .
而且確實 , 在老鼠蒐羅環境時 , 我們在海馬區的輸入訊號中 , 檢測到能對距環境邊界的特定距離與方向作出精確感應的神經元細胞 。	and indeed , in mice , when it comes to inputs in the hippocampus , we detect specific distances and directions that respond to precisely sensing neurons from the border of the environment .
這裡左邊的細胞 , 你可以看出 , 當老鼠向東靠近邊界或屏障時 , 該細胞都會作出反應 , 不論這邊界是一個方盒的邊還是一個圓柱盒的邊甚至是老鼠繞著轉的桌布的垂簾 。	the cell on the left here , as you can tell , is responding when the mouse approaches the east border or the barrier , whether it's a box or a column box or even a rotating tablecloth .
而右面的細胞則是在老鼠南面出現邊界時響應 , 不論這邊界是桌布的垂簾還是一堵牆甚至是兩個被隔開的桌子之間的間隙 。	and the cells on the right respond when the border appears on the south side of the mouse , whether it's the tablecloth curtain or the wall between two separated tables .
以上是我們所推測的一種 " 定位細胞 " 給動物定位的方式 。	so this is a way that we speculate about positioning cells for animals .
我們也可檢測 , 人類在簡單環境中 , 是怎樣給諸如這面旗這樣的物體定位的或者乾脆把這物體想成你的車 。	we can also detect how humans , in simple environments , position objects like this or just think of this object as your car .
我們先讓人們熟悉一下環境 , 同時記下物體所在的位置 。	let's get people familiar with the environment and remember where the objects are .
接著 , 再讓他們回到那個環境 , 通常他們都能根據記憶準確無誤地標出物體所在的位置 。	and then they return to that environment , and usually they're able to tag objects based on memory accurately where they are .
但在一些試驗中 , 我們會改變環境的形狀和尺度 , 正如我們在 " 定位細胞 " 實驗中所做的那樣 。	but in some trials , we change the shape and the scale of the environment , just like we did in the targeted cell experiment .
如此 , 我們可以透過研究實驗者改變環境的形狀和尺度 , 來了解旗幟發生了怎樣的位移	in this way , we can change the shape and scale of the environment by studying the experimenter to understand where the flag was shifting .
比如現在你所看到的 , 假設這面旗幟在如圖中小四方形內的 " × " 的位置 , 然後接著你問人們小旗在哪 , 但實際上你已經將總環境的尺度擴大了 , 結果他們所認為的旗所在的位置也相應地向外擴張 , 而這擴張的模式和 " 定位細胞 " 的一模一樣 。	what you're seeing now , if this flag is expanding in the location of the xx , as you see in the tiny square , and then you ask people where the flag is , but you actually scale up the scale of the environment , and it turns out that the flag is expanding in exactly the same way as the pattern of the position cell .
這就好像你是透過儲存被某一特定位置所激發的 " 定位細胞 " 產生的訊號模式來記憶小旗的位置的 , 接著當你回到那個地點的時候 , 透過四處打量 , 便可以將你當前腦中 " 定位細胞 " 的訊號模式與之前的模式進行匹配 。	it's as if you're storing the signal patterns that are fired by a specific location cell in a specific place to match the location of the flag , and then when you go back to that location , you can match the patterns of your brain with your previously patterned .
這個過程便可讓你回到 " 老地方 " 。	this process lets you go back to the old place .
我們也能透過位移來給自己定位 。	we can also give ourselves locations through our positions .
因此當我們外出時或許是我們停車後下來隨便走走我們可以給自己定位 , 因為我們可以粗略地將自己的運動路線與大體的返回方向進行整合 。	so when we're out , maybe when we park and we walk around , we can position ourselves , because we can integrate our own sports routes with our bodies back in the direction .
" 定位細胞 " 也能從一種叫做 " 網狀細胞 " 的細胞那兒獲得此類線路整合的資訊 。	position cells can also be integrated into information from a cell called net cells .
目前在向海馬區的訊號輸入中又發現了 " 網狀細胞 " , 它們與 " 定位細胞 " 有點類似 。	and what's currently discovered in the hippocampus is that net cells are a little bit like position cells .
隨著老鼠的 " 四處探索 " , 每一個神經元細胞被大量各種位置所激發的訊號組合在一起 , 貫穿整個環境構成一個令人驚歎的規整的三角網格 。	with mice , each neuron is assembled by massive amounts of positions , and throughout the environment , it's a remarkable triangle grid .
倘若你對一系列 " 網狀細胞 " 進行記錄這裡以不同的顏色區分每一個細胞發出的訊號都能形成網狀 , 遍及整個環境 , 而且每一個細胞的網狀訊號集的位置都與其他細胞有一定偏差 。	if you document a series of mesh cells in different colors , each cell's signal can form a mesh , all the way throughout the environment , and each cell's mesh is in some way delayed from the other cells .
因此紅色標註的細胞訊號集合在這個網格上 , 綠色的是這個 , 而藍色的是這個 。	so the signals that are shown in red are gathered on this grid , and green are this , and blue are this one .
因此綜合來看 , 這就好像老鼠可以在它所到達的環境中建立一個虛擬的位置訊號網這就有點像你在地圖上所看到的經線和緯線 , 只不過要將線替換成 " 三角形 " 。	so in synthesis , it's like a mice can create a virtual location network in its environment , which is kind of like the lines and latitudes that you see on the map , except instead of replacing the line with triangles .
當老鼠移動的時候 , 這些電訊號能透過這些細胞傳遞給下一個神經元細胞從而為老鼠定位 , 這樣老鼠就能在運動時知道自己身在何處 。	when the mouse is moving , these electrical signals can be delivered to the next neuron from these cells so that the mouse can know where they are in the motion .
那麼人類是否有 " 網狀細胞 " 呢 ?	so does humans have the mesh cells ?
因為所有的網狀訊號集合體都有相同的對稱軸 , 以及相同的網格朝向 , 這裡以橘紅色標識 , 這就意味著大腦中特定部位的所有網狀細胞的聯網行為的變化應該取決於我們是在向著這六個方向運動還是沿著六個方向之間所夾的某一個方向運動 。	because all the signals collectively have the same axes of symmetry and the same grid dynamics , and in this orange red identity , this means that the change in all the mesh cells in the brain depends on whether we're moving towards those six directions or whether we're moving in one direction between six directions .
我們可以為人們做核磁共振掃描 , 與此同時讓他們玩一個小型電子遊戲 , 還是之前所說的那個遊戲 , 然後來看看當時的訊號 。	we can do mri scans for people , and let them play a little video game , or that game , as i said before , and let's look at the signal .
啊哈沒錯 , 你在人腦中的內嗅皮層上看到了網狀細胞 , 而它們出現的位置和老鼠的網狀細胞在大腦中所出現的位置一樣 。	ahha is right , you see the net cells on the inside of the human brain , and they're just as positioned as the mesh cells of the mouse are in the brain .
現在我們回頭看看荷馬 。	now let's go back to homer .
他可能憑藉與周邊建築以及四周邊界的相對距離和方向來回憶他的車停在哪兒 。	he could recall where his car parked by relative distances and directions with surrounding buildings and surrounding them .
而那將由專門 " 檢測邊界 " 的神經元細胞發出的訊號來執行 。	and that will execute the signals from the neurons that specialize at the border .
他可能也記得自己是怎麼從停車場走出來的 , 而這就有賴於網狀細胞發出訊號了 。	and he probably remembers how he came out of the parking lot , and it relies online cells sending signals .
這兩種型別的神經元細胞都可以啟用 " 定位細胞 " 。	these two different types of neurons can be activated as " positioned cells . "
因此荷馬成功折返的方法便是在走動中尋求與他之前停車時腦中所建立的訊號集樣式最為匹配的一個腦中即時形成的訊號集樣式 。	and so the way homer's successful folding return works is by walking around seeking signals that were built in his previous parking brain , matching one of the most immediate brain signals that were formed in real time .
而那就能將他領回 " 老地方 " 了 , 這個過程與最終的目標視物無關不論他的車是否還在那兒他都能找到停車點 。	and that brings him back to the old place , which is not about the final target , whether he's still there or not , he can find the parking spot .
或許車已經被拖走了 ,	maybe the car has been dragged away .
但他仍然知道車原來停在哪 , 因此他會回到原位去取車 。	but he still knows where the car parked , so he goes back to where it was .
撇開 " 空間記憶力 " 而言 , 倘若我們單獨觀察這種網狀訊號集在整個大腦中的活動情況 , 就會發現這種訊號形式分佈廣泛 , 每當我們需要回憶一些自己過去的經歷時這種網狀的訊號形式就會活躍起來 , 譬如 , 當你試圖回憶上次參加婚禮的情況時	and aside from spatial memory , if we alone observe this signal gathering throughout the brain , this signal distributes widely distributed , every time we need to recall some of our experiences , this mesh form activates , like when you're trying to recall the previous wedding .
因此有可能 , 神經元細胞再現空間的功能也參與視覺畫面的呈現這樣當我們試圖回憶一個曾經置身其中的場面時 , 至少可以藉助想象而勾勒出整個場景 。	so it's possible that neurons reconstruct the function of space and participate in the visual appearance so that when we're trying to recall a scene that was once there , we can at least check the whole picture by imagining it .
倘若事實果真如此 , 記憶的形成就開始於: " 定位細胞 " 透過這些縝密的連結相互啟用然後 " 邊界感應細胞 " 被再次啟用從而形成我們視點周圍的場景的空間格局 。	and if that's true , the memory formation begins: " position cells " activate each other through these very carefully interconnected connections , and " border sensing cells " become reintroduced to the spatial grid that we see around us .
網狀細胞可以使視點穿透那個空間 。	the mesh cells can make their perspective through that space .
而另一種 " 方位細胞 " , 我之前沒有提到它 , 它們像指南針一樣 , 都是根據你的朝向來作出反應的 。	and the other digital cell , which i didn't mention earlier , they respond like a compass based on where you're headed .
它們可以明確你需要在腦中形成哪個方位的影象 , 就拿回憶婚禮情景來說 , 以上過程就能讓你回想起那一切 。	they can specifically image where you need to form in your head , take back the wedding scenario , and remind you of all that .
好了 , 以上就是在認知神經科學領域所開闢的新紀元 , 在這個領域中 , 我們開始嘗試從大腦中數以億計的單個神經元細胞的行為出發 , 來了解人類心理活動產生的過程 。 比如人們是如何記憶、想象甚至思考的	all right , so that's the new era in the cognitive neuroscience field , where we're starting to start from the behavior of hundreds of millions of individual neurons in the brain to understand how human psychological activity is produced , how people remember , think and even think .
謝謝各位 。	thank you .
想象一個由合作多部門 , 多政府 , 公私力量組成的全球安全 。 這不僅是開放安全支持者的幻想 , 而是jamesstavridis , 北約最高長官的設想 , 他從分享了從現代軍事史的生動瞬間到解釋了為什麼要靠修橋而不是修牆來構築未來安全 。	imagine a global security made by cooperation , multiple governments , publicprivate forces , which is not just the illusion of opensource supporters but the imagination of james staviss , the highest officer in northern journey , who , from the sharing of the dynamics of modern military history , explains why we need to build the future security instead of fixing the wall .

jamesstavridis:北約的最高長官如何看待全球安全	james stavildis: northern commissioner , how to look at global security .
我將要介紹一些開放式安全性問題 , 因為我們在21世紀已經離安全越來越近了 。	i'm going to show you some opensource security issues , because we're getting closer and closer to safety in the 21st century .
我們先回顧一下20世紀吧 , 然後我們就能瞭解安全這個概念是如何為我們而工作 。	let's go back to the 20th century , and then we can understand how this idea of security works for us .
這裡是verdun , 一個法國的戰場 , 就在北約在比利時總部的北邊 。	this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the headquarters in belgium .
1916年 , 在verdun這個戰場上 , 700000人在300天內被殺了 , 那就是差不多2000人一天 。	in 1916 , on verdun , in a battlefield , 7 , 000 people were killed in 300 days , almost 2 , 000 people a day .
咱們繼續往前看--20世紀的安全--看到二戰 , 我們看得到在斯大林格勒保衛戰 , 300天內有二百萬人戰死 。	let's move forward the 20thcentury security see world war ii , we can see the war in stalin gregler , 300 days after two million people died .
進入冷戰 , 我們繼續建造圍牆 。	we went into the cold war , and we continued to build walls .
我們從一戰的壕溝 , 到二戰的馬其頓防線 , 再到冷戰中的鐵幕 , 柏林牆 。	we went from the trenches of world war ii to the macedonian defense , to the iron curtains of the cold war , the berlin wall .
所以我今天的主題是為了完成 " 安全 " 這個目標 , 我們不建造牆 , 而建造橋 。	so my thesis today is to achieve safety , we don't build walls and we build bridges .
在歐洲有一個很著名的橋 。	there's a famous bridge in europe .
它在drina河上 , 是作家ivoandric的一個小說的主題 , 這部小說講述了如何在歐洲和巴爾幹地區最動盪的部分大量的牆被築起 。	it's on the drina river , a novel by the author iivo andric , and it describes the most turbulent part of the wall in europe and the balkans .
而最近 , 也就是在近十年 , 我們開始看到這些地區開始 , 儘管有些猶豫不決 , 逐漸融合在一起 。	and recently , in the last 10 years , we're starting to see these regions start , despite being hesitant and increasingly mixing together .
我想再次重申 , 開放式安全是關於聯絡國際的不同地區的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的 , 並且把它們透過戰略性溝通 , 在社交網上聯絡在一起 。	i want to reclaim that opensource security is about connecting international , interagency , private and public , and connecting them through strategic communication to social networks .
所以 , 接下來我將說一些為什麼我們需要那麼做 , 因為我們的共同目標正在受到威脅 , 而且是多方面的 , 同時沒有一種威脅能被透過築牆隔離解決 。	so i'm going to talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our common goals are being threatened , and they're multiple ways , and they don't have a threat to be resolved through wall
現在 , 很明顯我是一個水手 。	now , obviously i'm a sailor .
有一個船在印度洋上航行 。	there's a boat sailing on the indian ocean .
這個照片有什麼問題嗎 ?	what's wrong with this picture ?
在這個船上有蛇網環繞 。	there's a snake nets on this boat .
這是用來抵禦海盜的 。	this is used to defend pirates .
海盜現在是一個非常主要的全球威脅 。 這是隻是在印度洋 。	pirates are now a very primary global threat . this is an indian ocean .
海盜依然在馬六甲海峽很猖狂 ,	pirates are still rampant in the channels of mankind .
也在幾內亞灣 ,	it's in the gulf of guinea .
在加勒比海地區 。	it's in the caribbean .
它在全球交通運輸中每年造成了一百億美元的損失 。	it costs about 10 billion dollars a year to lose global transport .
在去年的此刻 , 有20艘船 , 500名船員被綁架為人質 。	at this point last year , 20 boats , 500 crew abducted into hostage .
這是一個對全球共同利益的威脅 。	it's a threat to global commons .
我們需要想出解決辦法 。	we need to come up with solutions .
現在讓我們轉到另一種海洋 , 網路的海洋 。	now let's move to another ocean , the internet's ocean .
這裡有兩個年輕人的照片 。	here's a picture of two young people .
在此刻 , 他們被監禁著 。	at this point , they're incarcerated .
他們做了一個信用卡詐騙案 , 並且牟利超過一百億美元 。	they made a credit card fraud for over 10 billion dollars .
這只是對全球經濟造成兩萬億美元損失的網路犯罪的一部分 。	this is part of cybercrime that costs 20 trillion dollars to the global economy .
兩萬億每年 。	two trillion dollars a year .
這僅低於英國的國民生產總值.	that's less than the gdp of the united kingdom .
所以網路世界 , 一個我們深知是由最根本的開放組成的地方 , 正在受到威脅 。	so the internet world , a place that we know is threatened by the most fundamental openness .
另一個我要擔心的是由於物流造成的威脅 , 也就是麻醉劑 , 鴉片等毒品從阿富汗穿過歐洲到達美國的整個一條運輸線 。	another thing i worry about is the threat caused by logistics , which is called anesthetics , opioids , which goes from afghanistan to europe to the united states .
我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因 。	we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .
我們擔心非法武器的運輸 。 但最重要的是 , 我們擔心人力的運輸 , 以及它的成本 。	we worry about illegal weapons transport , but most importantly , we worry about human transport and its cost .
大多數運輸是透過海洋的但也透過我們的共同利益 。	most of it is through the ocean , but through our common interests .
這是一張照片 , 透過它我想告訴你這是一個非常高科技的美國海軍武器用來阻止物流的發生 。	this is a photograph , and i'd like to tell you it's a very hightech navy weapon to stop logistics .
但壞訊息是 , 這是一個販毒組織的半潛水的裝置 。	but the bad news is , it's a semisubsory device that vends tissue .
它在南美熱帶雨林中被建造 ,	it was built in the rainforests of south america .
我們透過沒有科技含量的筏子逮捕了它 , 而它正裝載著六噸的可卡因 ,	we've arrested it with no technology raft , and it's carrying six tons of cocaine .
四個船員 , 精良的裝置 。	four crews , delicate installations .
這種運送麻醉劑 , 人和武器上帝禁止的 , 大規模殺傷性武器就是我們共同利益的威脅的一部分 。	this shipping anesthetic , human and weapons banned , and mass destruction is part of the threat of our collective interest .
現在讓我們完整的看一下阿富汗的今天 。	now let's take a full look at afghanistan today .
在阿富汗有一片罌粟花的 ,	there's a poppy in afghanistan .
全世界80%到90%的罌粟花 , 鴉片和海洛因來自阿富汗 。	eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppies , opium and heroin from afghanistan .
當然 , 我們也看到了恐怖組織 。	of course , we also saw terrorist organizations .
這就是基地組織建立的地方 。	this is where alqaeda is built .
我們看到了這裡有一個很不穩定的局勢 。	we see a very unstable situation here .
所以恐怖組織也是我們面臨的威脅的一部分 , 也是我們必須解決的 。	so terrorism is also part of our threat , and it's something we have to solve .
所以 , 在21世紀 ,	so , in the 21st century .
我們知道我們20世紀的方法不管用 。	we know that our 20thcentury method doesn't work .
我們該怎麼辦 ?	what do we do ?
我想說我們不能僅僅透過槍支來保障安全 。	i want to say that we cannot protect security just by guns .
我們不能僅僅依靠槍支 ,	we can't just rely on guns .
我們需要軍事力量的綜合應用 。	we need the application of military power .
當我們使用時 , 我們就必須使用好 。	when we're using it , we have to use it .
但我所要說的是 , 開放式安全是關於國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人和公共的聯絡 , 透過網際網路溝通而建立的 。	but all i'm saying is that opensource security is about international , interagency , private and public contact , and it's created through the internet .
讓我講一個例子 。	let me give you an example .
我們有阿富汗 , 有阿富汗計程車兵 ,	we have afghanistan . we have afghan taxi .
他們都拿著書 。	they're all holding books .
你可能會說 " 這真奇怪 , 我想我曾讀到過在這個地區絕大多數20 , 30多歲的年輕人都是不識字的 。 "	you might say , " that's strange , i think i've read that most young people in this area in their 20s and 30s are illiterate . "
你也許是對的 。	you might be right .
當他們進入安全部隊的時候 , 85%是不識字的 。	when they enter the security forces , 85 percent of them are illiterate .
為什麼 ? 因為塔利班在這些人該學習的時候不提供教育 。	why ? because the taliban are not providing education when these people are supposed to learn .
所以問題是 , 為什麼他們手裡拿著書站在那裡 ?	so the question is , why are they holding books in their hands ?
答案是 , 我們在叫他們閱讀 , 透過北約組織的課程 , 透過和私人組織的合作 , 透過和發展署的合作 。	and the answer is , we're asking them to read through the northern organization program , through collaboration with private organizations , through collaboration with development agencies .
我們已經教了超過200000的阿富汗安全部隊士兵來進行最基本的讀寫 。	we've taught more than 2 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at the most basic level .
當你能讀和寫的時候 , 你就會在你的口袋裡放一支筆 。	when you can read and write , you put a pen in your pocket .
在畢業典禮上 , 當這些人畢業時 , 他們很驕傲的拿出筆 , 並放在他們的口袋裡 。	at the ceremony , when these people graduated , they were proud to take the pen and put it in their pocket .
這個舉動把全世界有五十個國家跨部門的力量私人和公共資源都聯絡到了一起 , 來進行這種安全的建立 。	this has connected the power of 50 countries all over the world to private and public resources to do this kind of security .
現在 , 我們當然也教他們格鬥技巧 , 但我想說 , 開放式安全意味著為創造更持久的安全而聯絡各個力量 。	now , we also teach them fighting techniques , but i want to say that opensource security means connecting with forces to create longer lasting security .
這是一個美國海軍戰艦 。	this is a us navy warship .
叫做comfort號 。	it's called the comfort .
他有一個姊妹艦 , 叫做mercy號 。	he had a sistership called the mercy .
他們是友好的戰艦 。	they're friendly battleships .
安慰號在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。	the comfort in the caribbean and the coast of south america conducted patient treatment .
通常 , 他會進行400000個治療 ,	typically , he ran 4 , 000 treatments .
船員不是嚴格的部隊人員 , 而是很多人道主義組織 , 比如 " 希望專案 " , " 微笑工程 " 。	crew was not a strict military , but a lot of people said , " hope project , " " " smile engineering . "
其他組織送來志願者 。	other organizations send volunteers .
其他部門的醫生也來了 。	so doctors from other sectors have come .
他們都是這個專案的一部分 。	they're all part of this project .
舉個例子來說明這個專案的影響力 , 這個小孩 , 8歲 , 和他的媽媽走了兩天來到安慰號上的眼科診所 。	to give you an example of the impact of this project , this kid , eight years old , walked with his mother for two days to come to eye clinic on comfort .
當他被治好他的重度近視是 , 他突然抬頭 , 然後說: " mama , veoelmundo. "	when he was healed , he looked up , and he said , " mama , veo elmundo . "
" 媽媽 , 我看到世界了 。 "	" mom , i see the world . "
把這個乘以400000 , 也就是治療數目 , 這個私人和公共的合作 , 同時融合了安全力量的專案 , 開始顯現它的力量 , 來以一個很不同的方式創造安全 。	multiply this by 400 , 000 , which is the number of treatments , this private and public collaboration that integrates the power of security and begins to show its power to create security in a very different way .
這張照片是棒球運動員 。	this is a baseball player .
你能在其中找出兩名美國部隊計程車兵嗎 ?	can you find two american taxi military taxi military in between ?
他們是每側最邊上的兩位 。 這是棒球診所的一部分 , 在這裡我們嘗試棒球聯賽 , 國務院 , 在軍隊中的棒球運動員 , 也就是那些能真正上戰場的人 , 之間的合作 , 並且他們把這種診所開到了拉丁美洲和加勒比地區 , 開到了宏都拉斯 , 開到了尼加拉瓜 , 開到了所有中美洲和加勒比的棒球很流行國家 , 而且它創造了安全感 。	they're the two people on each side . this is part of a baseball clinic , where we tried baseball leagues , state department , baseball players in the military , who actually went to war , collaborated with each other , and they opened this clinic to latin america and the caribbean , to honduras , to open nicaragua , to all the central american and caribbean baseball country pandemic , to create a sense of security .
他為年輕人建立了關於健身和生活的榜樣 , 而且我想說這些理念幫助創造了安全 。	he built role models for young people , and i would say these ideas helped create security .
這個合作的另一部分是災後救援與後續工作 。	another part of this collaboration is after disaster rescue and subsequent work .
這是一個美國空軍的直升機 , 它參加了2004年一個殺死250000人的海嘯的救援 。	this is a u . s . air force helicopter participating in a tsunami rescue that killed 25 , 000 people in 2004 .
在所有的大災難中2004年海嘯 , 250000死 , 2005年巴基斯坦地震 , 85000人死亡 , 海地地震 , 300000人死亡 , 還有最近的對於日本機器核工業的地震海嘯雙重打擊在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間 , 跨部門 , 公私結合的合作 , 這個合作與安全力量同時響應這種自然災害 。	tsunami in 2004 , 25 , 000 dead , the crossborder earthquake in pakistan in 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , 3 , 000 dead , and more recently , to the earthquake of the japanese nuclear industry , in all of these examples , we've seen international , interagency , privatepublic collaboration with security forces that respond to natural disaster .
所以這些都是我們說的開放式安全的例子 。	so these are examples of what we call opensource security .
我們結合在一起 , 來共同完成這樣的事情 。	we combined to do something like this together .
現在你看到這個 , 應該在想 , " 啊 , 船長 , 這些一定是通訊電纜 , 或者是光線 。 "	now you're looking at this and you're thinking , " ah , ship captain , these must be communication cables , or light . "
不 , 這是一個twitter公司發的世界地圖 。	no , this is a world map of twitter .
紫色是微博 , 綠色是地點 ,	purple is microblog , and green is location .
白色是結合 。	white is combination .
這很能讓人想到人口普查 , 六個人口最多的國家依次是:中國 , 印度 , facebook , 美國 , twitter , 和印尼 。	it's reminiscent of the census , and the six largest population remains: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter , and indonesia .
我們要這些網幹什麼 ?	what do we want these nets to do ?
我們為什麼想要在其中 ?	why do we want to be there ?
我們之前討論過阿拉伯春天組織 , 以及它的力量 。	we talked earlier about the arab spring and its power .
我再舉一個例子 , 是關於資訊如何傳播的 。	i'll give you another example of how information is spreading .
我在倫敦發表一個像這個的演講 。 我說 , 我對你們說 , 我在facebook上 , 加我好友吧 。	i gave a talk like this in london , and i said , " i'm on facebook . "
觀眾在笑 。	audiences are laughing .
這是ap的一篇文章 。	this is an article by ap .
世界上有兩個地方 , 芬蘭和印尼 ,	there are two places in the world , finland and indonesia .
標題是:北約艦隊司令需要好友 。	the headline: northern journey commands need friends .
這個故事是一個催化劑 , 明天早上我就會有上百個facebook好友請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭 , 大多數都會說: " 司令 , 我們聽說你需要好友 , 哦 , 還有 , nato是什麼 ? "	this story is a catalyst , and tomorrow morning i have hundreds of facebook friends requests from indonesia and finland , mostly saying , " command , we heard you need a friend , and , oh , what is nato ? "
是的 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何傳播資訊 , 也就是我們如何把國際 , 不同部門 , 私人和公共 , 以及那些社會網聯絡起來來創造安全 。	yes , we laughed , but that's how we communicate information , how we make international , different sectors , private and public , and those social networks connect to create security .
現在 , 讓我說一個嚴肅的訊息 。	now , let me tell you a serious message .
這是一個勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。	this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .
他在蘇格蘭衛隊 ,	he was in the scottish guards .
正在helmand站崗 , 在阿富汗南部 。	he's standing there in helmand , in southern afghanistan .
我把他放出來就是想提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開這間屋子 , 抱著 " 我們不需要軍事部隊 " 的想法 。	and i put him out there just to remind us that i don't want anyone to leave this room with the idea that we don't need the military .
這正是我們在做的 , 我們做這個事情來保障自由 , 言論自由 , 和其他所有我們在社會中珍視的 。	and that's exactly what we do , and we do this to protect freedom , freedom of speech , and all the other things that we value in our society .
但你知道 , 生活不是開關 。	but you know , life is not a switch .
我們沒有要麼在戰爭 , 要麼在兵營的軍事力量 。	we're not either in a war or in a military .
我認為生活是一個可變電阻器 ,	i think life is a defibrillator .
你需要調一個數值 , 並且正像我認為我們該如何在21世紀製造安全一樣 , 我們會需要在真正的戰爭和危機中使用真正強硬的力量 , 但會有很多時候 , 就像我們已經討論的 , 我們的部隊可以使21世紀安全 , 也就是國際 , 跨部門 , 公私結合 , 的安全模式的一部分 , 透過溝通來結合起來 。	you need to address a score , and just as i think we're making security in the 21st century , we're going to need to use really hard power in real war and crisis , but there's going to be a lot of times , and as we've been talking about , our troops can get 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic patterns , combined with communication .
在結束時 , 我想說在今天早些時候聽到的關於維基百科的一些東西 。 我經常用維基百科查一些東西 , 就像你所知道的 , 維基百科不是靠12個聰明的人把自己關在屋子裡寫文章建立的 。	so to close , i want to say that earlier today , i've heard about wikipedia , and i've often used wikipedia to look at things , as you know , wikipedia isn't built by 12 brilliant people in the room .
維基百科是靠每天數萬人的更新 , 數百萬人的提取資訊而建立的 。	wikipedia is built every day by updating tens of thousands of people , by extracting information from millions of people .
這完美的說明了沒有一個人能比共同思考更聰明 。	it's a perfect illustration that nobody is smarter than thinking together .
沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 能有我們共同思考更睿智 。	none of us , none of us , none of our allies , no country , can think together much wiser .
維基百科的宣言很簡單:建立一個能人人自由共享所有知識的世界 。	the statement of wikipedia is simple: create a world free to share all knowledge .
所以 , 我想說 , 透過結合國際 , 多部門 , 公私力量 , 戰略通訊在一起 , 在21世紀 , 我們能創造共同的安全 。	so i would like to say that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communications together , we can create shared security in the 21st century .
非常感謝 。	thank you very much .
